Key placement & consistency checks
• All objects sit flush on floor (y = height·0.5 for desks/chairs; fixed in the y-positions above).  
• No object intersects walls: maximum X (7.1 m) < right-wall inner face (8 m) and minimum X (0.05 m) > left-wall inner face (0 m).  
• Back-row items (z ≤ 5.95 m) clear the back wall (6 m).  
• Ceiling lights at y = 3 m are just below wall height (3 m).  
• Chairs rotated 180° to face whiteboard/front wall.  
• Bookshelf and window correctly anchored to right wall; posters to left/back walls.  
• Dinosaur skeleton placed safely in back-left corner without clipping bookshelf.
